We all love those motivational shorts and videos on YouTube and Instagram, right? But have you noticed the latest trend? Animated motivational stories are taking over, and they're not only captivating but also highly lucrative. In today's video, I'm going to show you how you can create these popular animated stories using AI tools. Let's dive in!

Introduction
Animated motivational stories are a hit on social media. Channels dedicated to this niche are gaining thousands of subscribers quickly. For instance:

One channel with just 20 videos has 63K subscribers.
Another with 30 videos has over 85K subscribers.
Yet another boasts over 1 million subscribers!
Hardly anyone is talking about how to create these videos using AI. That changes today.

Why This Niche?

Motivational shorts niche is saturated.
Animated stories are relatively untapped.
Sharing content on multiple platforms (YouTube, Facebook, Instagram, TikTok) increases success chances.
Step 1: Crafting an Engaging Story

Use ChatGPT to generate a short moral and motivational story (around 350 words).
Provide a reference story to ensure the format matches your needs.
Simplify the language if needed to make it more engaging.
Alternative: Search for motivational stories on Google.

Step 2: Generating AI Images

Ask ChatGPT to generate image prompts for each line of your story.
Use Playground AI or Ideogram AI to create stunning images based on these prompts.
Adjust settings like the number of images and dimensions to get the best results.
Step 3: Creating a Short Animated Video

Use Haiper AI video generator (currently free in beta version).
Copy the video prompts from ChatGPT and paste them into Haiper AI.
Choose your animation style (e.g., 3D animation, Disney style, vector style).
Step 4: Adding Voice-Over

Use Eleven Labs for high-quality voice generation.
Customize the voice to suit your story.
If Eleven Labs isn't accessible, use TTS Maker AI as a free alternative.
Step 5: Editing the Video

Use Capcut or Wondershare Filmora to bring everything together.
Import your voice-over, images, and videos into the timeline.
Sync the story with the visuals.
Add filters, effects, and animations to make your video more engaging.
Generate subtitles and customize them.
Add background music from YouTube's audio library to avoid copyright issues.
Conclusion

Create captivating animated motivational stories that stand out and attract a large audience.
Share your videos across multiple platforms to maximize your reach.
Grab a glass of mango juice and enjoy the process. Letâ€™s get started with step 1: crafting your story. Watch the full video to learn all the secrets and tips!
